**§11.4.170 — Device-independent host-side rendered-UI visual-proof mandate (User mandate, 2026-06-25).** Every change to any user-facing UI surface (screen/component/view/widget/layout/theme on any platform — Android-Compose, iOS-SwiftUI/UIKit, web, desktop, TUI) MUST be proven by DEVICE-INDEPENDENT host-side RENDERED PIXELS before it may be claimed correct: the actual component rendered to a PNG ON THE HOST (NO device, NO emulator, NO running app; Compose→Roborazzi/Paparazzi, web→Playwright/Storybook, SwiftUI→snapshot-testing, equiv per stack) for EVERY `screen × state × {light,dark}` theme, dual-validated by (i) golden image-diff AND (ii) an OCR/vision oracle reading rendered text + labels + control bounds (NO overlap / label-over-label / clipping / off-screen / collapsed-or-giant-unbounded widget — the §11.4.162 layout invariants PROVEN on real pixels). Forbidden bluff (forensic FACT 2026-06-25): UI "validated" by VALUE/token/property-equality unit tests (a hex colour string, an sp/dp integer, a design-token field == a constant) that NEVER RENDERED A PIXEL stayed GREEN while the operator opened a broken giant-button screen — value/token/property-equality UI tests are FORBIDDEN as the PROOF a UI is correct (may SUPPLEMENT, NEVER SUBSTITUTE the rendered-pixel proof); a green UI suite with no rendered-pixel artefact for the changed surface is a §11.4 PASS-bluff. ALL hold: rendered-pixel proof per screen×state×theme, run on EVERY commit with zero hardware; dual oracle both required, each PASS citing the captured PNG + diff (§11.4.5/§11.4.69); a value-only UI claim is a §11.4.4 finding → render → fix → re-render GREEN; self-validated analyzer golden-good/golden-bad (§11.4.107(10)), thresholds on the project's OWN fixtures (§11.4.6); "device offline" is NEVER a valid skip (host-render IS the device-independent path); genuine no-host-render-harness ⇒ honest §11.4.3 SKIP + tracked migration item, never a value-only fallback. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): host-render proves the component renders correctly device-independently on every commit — it COMPLEMENTS not replaces §11.4.153/§11.4.158/§11.4.159/§11.4.160 live-device recording + §11.4.162 OpenDesign tokens + §11.4.168 exported-doc visual validation. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-170-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.170`) + recommended gate `CM-HOST-RENDERED-UI-VISUAL-PROOF` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.170. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--value-assertion-proves-ui`, `--skip-rendered-pixel-proof`, `--token-equality-suffices`, `--device-offline-skip-visual`, `--single-theme-only`, `--unvalidated-image-diff-OK`, `--no-ocr-layout-oracle` flag.

**§11.4.171 — Mandatory comprehensive human-readable workable-item descriptions (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** Every workable item (ATM-NNN ticket) in the project's workable-items database, Issues.md, Fixed.md, Issues_Summary.md, Fixed_Summary.md, and ALL derived documents MUST carry a comprehensive human-readable description in plain, non-technical language suitable for non-developers (project managers, stakeholders, team leads, business partners) — ≥ 5-7 sentences covering (a) WHAT it is (feature/fix/task in simple terms); (b) WHY it matters (user/business value); (c) HOW it works (mechanism, no code references); (d) WHO benefits; (e) the expected measurable outcome. Jargon, unexpanded acronyms, code references, and implementation details are FORBIDDEN as the primary explanation (technical detail may appear as supplementary context AFTER the plain-language explanation). An item without a human-readable description is a §11.4 documentation-layer violation. The `description` column in the SQLite DB (`docs/workable_items.db`) is the SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH; all derived documents carry the SAME description text. Gate `CM-HUMAN-READABLE-DESCRIPTION` (when implemented) asserts every item's `description` exists, non-empty, ≥ 50 characters; paired §1.1 mutation strips a description → gate FAILs. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.15 / §11.4.16 / §11.4.19 / §11.4.91 / §11.4.93 / §11.4.148 / §11.4.65. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-171-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.171`) + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.171. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.172 — Mandatory production-readiness planning with realistic timeline projection (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** Every project under this Constitution MUST maintain a living production-readiness planning document that: (a) provides REALISTIC timeline projections for all milestones (MVP, beta, production-ready) based on actual development velocity data (items completed per week, reopening rate, blocking dependencies); (b) identifies ALL danger zones, weaknesses, and risk areas with mitigation strategies; (c) accounts for HW-delivery timelines, licensing delays, and external-dependency risks; (d) defines the critical path and which items can slip without affecting MVP; (e) includes workstation/build-capacity analysis + optimization recommendations; (f) is updated at least monthly or whenever the item count changes by ≥ 10%; (g) is cross-referenced against the workable-items database for accuracy. The document lives at `docs/research/production_planning_<YYYYMMDD>/ANALYSIS.md` with HTML+PDF exports per §11.4.65. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): projections are velocity-based estimates — they guarantee sound methodology, NOT that specific dates will be met. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.6 / §11.4.40 / §11.4.42 / §11.4.93 / §11.4.108. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-172-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.172`) + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.172. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.173 — Containerized + distributed build mandate (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** EVERY build of EVERY component (source compile, artifact/package/installer/container-image production, codegen, asset render — for ANY language/platform: Go, Android/Gradle, desktop, web, native, firmware) MUST run INSIDE a specialized build container provisioned via the `digital.vasic.containers` submodule (§11.4.76) — NEVER on the bare host. The build containers MUST be DISTRIBUTED to the designated remote build host(s) via the SAME containers-submodule distribution mechanism (remote compose over SSH §11.4.76, rootless §11.4.161) so the build EXECUTES on the remote host (offloading the developer/main host); once complete the produced artifacts MUST be brought BACK to the originating host (scp/rsync/volume copy) for use/flashing/distribution. Building outside a container, or on the bare host, is FORBIDDEN — a release blocker (the "works on my machine" / unreproducible-build class). Build-host target + build-container definitions are config-injected (§11.4.28, never hardcoded in the submodule); a missing build-container capability is added by EXTENDING the containers submodule upstream (§11.4.74), never an ad-hoc host build. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): the containerized + distributed build guarantees reproducibility + host-isolation + capacity offload — it does NOT replace the §11.4.40 full-suite retest, §11.4.108 artifact→runtime verification, or §11.4.38 installable-asset evidence on the brought-back artifact. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.76 / §11.4.161 / §11.4.74 / §11.4.28 / §11.4.24 / §11.4.82 / §11.4.121 / §11.4.38 / §11.4.108 / §12.6. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-173-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.173`) + recommended gate `CM-CONTAINERIZED-DISTRIBUTED-BUILD` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.173. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--build-on-host`, `--skip-container-build`, `--local-build-ok`, `--no-distributed-build`, `--bare-host-build` flag.

**§11.4.174 — Shared-host process-ownership verification mandate (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** Verbatim operator mandate: "Make sure that processes we are checking are always OURS! ... on every host there may be other work being done!" On ANY host where concurrent work from other projects / users / agents may run (the normal case — a shared developer workstation), EVERY inspection of, conclusion about, or action on a process, build, daemon, port, lock-file, or system-state signal MUST FIRST positively VERIFY the target is OURS before drawing a diagnosis or acting. A diagnosis based on another project's process is a §11.4.6 guessing error; KILLING / signalling / restarting / altering a process that is NOT positively ours is a §12 + §11.4.133 safety violation (operator-workload destruction) — forbidden. Forensic FACT (2026-06-29): a 200%-CPU `java` + `gradlew` on the shared host was nearly mis-attributed to our build but was a separate `catalogizer` project's gradle test (`cwd=Projects/catalogizer`); a naive `pgrep java`/`gradle` would have matched it as "ours." ALL hold: (a) positive-ownership discriminator REQUIRED — attribute to us ONLY via a strong signal: `cwd` resolving inside THIS project's tree, `argv` naming our scripts/artifacts/repo path, a PID we launched + recorded (§11.4.147 registry), or a lock/port/socket path under our tree; a loose name match (`pgrep java`/`gradle`/`node`/`python`/`podman`/`zig`) is NEVER sufficient; (b) NEVER kill/signal/restart a process not positively ours — other projects' daemons/pods are off-limits; the §12.8 `pkill -f GradleDaemon` remediation MUST be scoped to OUR daemons (cwd/argv under our tree), never host-wide; (c) contention → surface, don't break (§11.4.66 / §11.4.101), keep progressing non-blocked work; (d) every `pgrep`/`ps` filter MUST exclude the checking command's OWN argv AND other-project matches, preferring our absolute repo path; (e) applies to ALL state (ports, lock files, caches, pods, tmux sessions, temp files), not just processes. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): ownership-verified inspection prevents mis-attribution + cross-project damage — it does not itself prove our process is healthy. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.6 / §11.4.101 / §11.4.66 / §11.4.147 / §12 / §12.8 / §11.4.133. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-174-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.174`) + recommended gate `CM-PROCESS-OWNERSHIP-VERIFIED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.174. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--assume-process-ours`, `--loose-pgrep-ok`, `--kill-any-matching-process`, `--skip-ownership-check` flag.

**§11.4.176 — Conflict-free multi-track work-division + exactly-once claim registry + capability-aware deadlock-proof device-lock (User mandate, 2026-07-02).** When a project runs multiple concurrent work-STREAM tracks (§11.4.167 / §11.4.58 / §11.4.103) sharing (a) a common pool of workable items and (b) a scarce pool of exclusive hardware/resources, TWO cooperating arbitration layers are MANDATORY, both conflict-free BY CONSTRUCTION: **(A) work-item layer — exactly-once claim registry** — every workable item OR logical GROUP of items sharing files/subsystem/feature/schema is assigned to AT MOST ONE track at a time via a lock-arbitrated append-only claim registry (extends §11.4.147 + §11.4.116); claim-before-touch, a second claim on an already-claimed item is DENIED; logical groups are claimed WHOLE (disjoint file-scope §11.4.58 L3 + per-track worktree/CoW §11.4.167 = tracks physically cannot touch the same bytes); no codebase loss (§9.2 backups / §11.4.113 ff-only-merge-onto-latest-main NEVER force-push / §11.4.84 quiescence / §11.4.41 merge-first); results ALWAYS produced (abandoned claim TTL-expires back to the pool). **(B) hardware layer — capability-aware deadlock-proof device-lock** — when N tracks outnumber M exclusive devices, exactly ONE track owns each device (§11.4.119); a track leases ONE OR MORE devices selected by required CAPABILITY (not merely identity); the arbiter is DEADLOCK-FREE by breaking all four Coffman conditions (hold-and-wait eliminated — multi-device acquire is ALL-OR-NOTHING in one critical section; circular-wait eliminated — acquire is NON-BLOCKING, wins the whole set or returns EBUSY; no-preemption relaxed — lease TTL + heartbeat + reap so a crashed holder's lease auto-expires §11.4.147; the only lock held is a short bounded flock over the atomic check-and-claim); registry = append-only JSONL + atomically-rewritten snapshot (§11.4.116). **(C) universal decoupling + evidence-based resource-tuning** — both layers universal/decoupled/project-not-aware (§11.4.17/§11.4.28/§11.4.35); resource-tuning decisions (stream count, per-stream memory §12.6, lease breadth, queue depth §11.4.167) MUST be EVIDENCE-BASED (§11.4.24 / §11.4.5), never guessed (§11.4.6). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.6/§11.4.17/§11.4.24/§11.4.28/§11.4.35/§11.4.41/§11.4.58/§11.4.84/§11.4.85/§11.4.103/§11.4.113/§11.4.116/§11.4.119/§11.4.147/§11.4.167/§12.6/§9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-176-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.176`) + recommended gates `CM-WORK-DIVISION-EXCLUSIVE-CLAIM` / `CM-NO-CROSS-TRACK-SCOPE-OVERLAP` / `CM-LOGICAL-GROUP-COHESION` / `CM-DEVICE-LOCK-DEADLOCK-FREE` + paired §1.1 mutations. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.176. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--allow-cross-track-overlap`, `--skip-claim-registry`, `--split-logical-group`, `--blocking-device-acquire`, `--allow-partial-device-hold`, `--tune-resources-by-guess` flag.

**§11.4.177 — Developer-tooling project-decoupling + invocation-directory operation (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** No project-specific script / hook / alias / binary may be wired — copied, symlinked, PATH-exported, or aliased — into a global or shared developer-tooling PATH; shared tooling MUST be project-agnostic and operate on the INVOCATION directory (cwd, or an explicit path/config argument), NEVER a hardcoded project path. A project-specific helper lives in + runs from its own repo; a genuinely-reusable helper is promoted to the shared toolkit ONLY after being stripped of every project-specific assumption (paths, device serials, package names, region endpoints) and taking its target from the invocation context. A project script reachable on the global/shared PATH is a decoupling violation of equal severity to importing project-specific code into a shared submodule (§11.4.28). Forensic FACT (2026-07-04): a project cwd-hook symlinked into the global Claude-Toolkit PATH re-coupled every alias to one hardcoded checkout. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): decoupling guarantees the tool is project-agnostic — NOT that it is correct (that still needs the tool's own tests). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.28 / §11.4.29 / §11.4.35 / §11.4.11 / §11.4.6. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-177-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.177`) + recommended gate `CM-TOOLING-PROJECT-DECOUPLED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.177. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--global-symlink-ok`, `--hardcode-project-path`, `--wire-into-shared-path` flag.

**§11.4.178 — Track-qualified identity for parallel work streams (session-name collision ban) (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** Parallel work streams that share hardware, a git backing store, a tmux/session namespace, a lock namespace, or any single-owner resource MUST be addressed by a TRACK-QUALIFIED identity (`<project>__<track>__<role>`), NEVER a bare directory basename. Multiple checkouts/clones/worktrees sharing basename `atmosphere` collapse into one session/lock/log key and cross-wire tmux targets, lock files, device claims, and log directories (the observed collision, 2026-07-04). Every registry row, session name, lock path, log directory, and device claim MUST carry the track-qualified key; a bare-basename identity for a resource with ≥ 2 concurrent claimants is a violation. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): a unique identity prevents cross-wiring — it does not itself arbitrate ownership (that is §11.4.119 + §11.4.176, the multi-track work-division + exactly-once-claim + device-lock arbitration anchor). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.111 / §11.4.119 / §11.4.176 / §11.4.29 / §11.4.58. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-178-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.178`) + recommended gate `CM-TRACK-QUALIFIED-IDENTITY` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.178. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--bare-basename-ok`, `--skip-track-qualifier`, `--shared-session-name` flag.

**§11.4.179 — Corruption-isolated parallel git streams (own-.git independent clones, not shared-common-dir worktrees) (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** When corruption-isolation is a requirement, parallel git work streams MUST each be an isolated repository with its OWN `.git` (own object store, own index, own lock namespace), NOT `git worktree` checkouts sharing one common `.git`. A shared common-dir is a single point of failure: one stale `index.lock` / `.commit_all.lock` / `.push_all.lock` freezes EVERY stream at once (the observed 9-h all-track freeze, 2026-07-04), and one corrupted object store loses every stream. Each stream's `git rev-parse --git-common-dir` MUST resolve INSIDE the stream's own tree; a common-dir resolving to a shared parent is a violation. Where CoW/reflink disk-feasibility is the constraint, use the §11.4.167 reflink-clone-with-own-`.git` path (a btrfs/XFS/ZFS/APFS reflink shares extents on disk while keeping a per-stream `.git`, so isolation and disk-feasibility both hold). Honest boundary (§11.4.6): own-`.git` isolation contains lock/corruption blast radius — it does NOT remove per-repo stale-lock reaping (§11.4.180) nor ff-only no-force integration (§11.4.113). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.167 / §11.4.119 / §11.4.176 / §11.4.58 / §9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-179-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.179`) + recommended gate `CM-GIT-STREAMS-OWN-COMMON-DIR` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.179. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--shared-common-git`, `--worktree-when-isolation-required`, `--skip-git-isolation` flag.

**§11.4.180 — Commit/push (single-writer) wrappers MUST auto-reap provably-stale locks before acquiring (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** Every commit / push / single-writer wrapper MUST, before acquiring its own lock, auto-reap any PROVABLY-stale git lock — one whose recorded holder PID is DEAD (`kill -0` fails), OR (no PID recorded) older than a defined threshold AND with no live wrapper/git process holding that repo. The reap covers the wrapper's own lock plus the git-internal existence-based locks (`index.lock`, `HEAD.lock`, `refs/**/*.lock`) that git does NOT auto-release on holder death. It MUST NEVER remove a lock whose holder is ALIVE (removing a live-held lock corrupts a concurrent writer — §9.2). Each reap decision (REAPED / KEPT + reason) is logged as captured evidence (§11.4.6 — liveness PROVEN via `kill -0`, never assumed). A wrapper that blocks indefinitely on a dead-holder lock (the observed 9-h freeze, 2026-07-04) is a violation. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): reaping clears dead-holder deadlock — it does NOT substitute for the own-`.git` isolation of §11.4.179 (which shrinks the blast radius from all-streams to one). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.84 / §11.4.88 / §11.4.6 / §9.2 / §11.4.116 / §11.4.179. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-180-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.180`) + recommended gate `CM-WRAPPER-STALE-LOCK-AUTO-REAP` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.180. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--skip-stale-lock-reap`, `--force-remove-live-lock`, `--block-on-dead-holder` flag.

**§11.4.181 — Consistent controlled feature-branch naming: one feature/logic-group ⇒ exactly ONE canonical branch name across the main repo + all owned submodules (User mandate, 2026-07-05).** Verbatim (2026-07-05): "System MUST pay attention not to create multiple feat. branches with different names for one same feature or group of workable items / features! Naming MUST BE consistent and carefully controlled!" One feature / logical group of workable items MUST map to EXACTLY ONE canonical branch name, used IDENTICALLY on the main repo AND every touched owned submodule — NEVER two differently-named branches for one feature/group, NEVER per-repo naming drift. ALL hold: (1) **single canonical name per group** minted ONCE per the §11.4.167 D scheme (`feature/<slug>` branch + `<prefix>-<base>-feat-<slug>` tag, `<slug>` lowercase snake/kebab §11.4.29), used identically across the main repo + every branched submodule (an untouched submodule stays on its base branch, NOT force-branched); (2) **single source of truth** — the canonical name is recorded ONCE in the §11.4.176 exactly-once claim registry / the §11.4.93 workable-items `logic_group → branch` mapping and LOOKED UP, never re-invented (creating a branch whose name ≠ the group's registered canonical name, OR minting a 2nd name for a group that already has one, is a §11.4.6 no-guessing violation); (3) **mechanical enforcement** (§11.4.75) — gate `CM-BRANCH-NAME-CONSISTENCY` FAILs on an unregistered feature-branch name / two divergent names for one group / a submodule branch diverging from the group's main-repo canonical name, paired §1.1 mutation (register one group under two divergent names → gate FAILs); (4) **risk-free reconciliation** (§9.2 / §11.4.113 / §11.4.84) — a mis-named/duplicate branch is reconciled by MERGING its commits onto the canonical branch (union, no `-s ours`/rebase/reset that drops commits, `git log <canonical>..<misnamed>` empty after merge, no conflict markers), ff-only push to all upstreams (NEVER force-push), retiring the mis-named branch only after the merge is confirmed on all mirrors (delete-before-merge forbidden). Honest boundary (§11.4.6): "probably the same feature" is NOT a determination — bind the branch to a group via the registry, never guess. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.167 / §11.4.176 / §11.4.178 / §11.4.179 / §11.4.28 / §11.4.29 / §11.4.93 / §11.4.113 / §11.4.84 / §11.4.6 / §11.4.75 / §9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-181-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.181`) + recommended gate `CM-BRANCH-NAME-CONSISTENCY` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.181. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--allow-divergent-branch-names`, `--skip-branch-registry`, `--rename-branch-freely`, `--per-repo-branch-name-OK`, `--two-names-one-feature-OK` flag.

**§11.4.182 — Track+branch work-stream identity label `(T<N>/<branch> - <alias>)` on every agent/subagent label + every operator-facing work-stream reference (User mandate, 2026-07-05).** Operator mandate (2026-07-05): "EVERY agent/subagent/work-stream label AND every operator-facing report reference to a work stream MUST carry a `(T<N>/<branch> - <alias>)` prefix identifying the track + git branch + the claude-toolkit alias in use — e.g. `(T1/main - claude1) ATM-312 MPV drm_prime investigation`, `(T2/feat/mistiq-vader - deepseek) SPK-XXX ...`." In a multi-track layout (parallel checkouts each on a distinct branch and potentially driven by a distinct claude-toolkit alias — e.g. `/mnt/track1..4`) a bare work-stream label does not say WHICH track/branch/alias produced it, so cross-track dispatches, status reports, and progress lines collide and mislead. ALL hold: (1) **universal label form** — every agent / subagent / work-stream label AND every operator-facing reference (agent-dispatch descriptions, status reports, resume/handoff docs, progress lines) MUST START with a `(T<N>/<branch> - <alias>)` prefix; (2) **deterministic derivation, never guessed** (§11.4.6) — `<N>` from the checkout path (`/mnt/track<N>/…`; honest `?` when not under a numbered track, never a guessed number), `<branch>` from `git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD`, `<alias>` from the `CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR` basename `.claude-<alias>` → `<alias>` (honest `?` when unset/non-matching, never a guessed name) (reference labeler `scripts/multitrack/track_branch_label.sh`); (3) **mechanical enforcement** (§11.4.75 / §11.4.109-class) — a PreToolUse guard hook (`constitution/scripts/hooks/guard-track-branch-label.sh`, inherited BY REFERENCE per §11.4.177, never copied) BLOCKS any Agent/Task/TaskCreate dispatch whose `description` (or `subagent` label) does not START with `^\(T[0-9]+/[^ )]+ - [^ )]+\) ` (branch AND alias both required, both non-empty), non-agent tools untouched; pre-build gate `CM-TRACK-BRANCH-LABEL` asserts labeler + hook exist/executable/parseable, hook wired in runtime settings, convention doc exists; (4) **honest boundary** (§11.4.6) — a `?` in the track field OR the alias field is a valid honest label (unknown track / no git repo / no matching `CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR`), never a bluff; the enforced format surfaces (blocks) an off-track dispatch or a dispatch missing its alias segment rather than silently mislabeling it. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.178 (the label-prefix instantiation applied to EVERY agent/subagent label + operator-facing reference) / §11.4.29 / §11.4.75 / §11.4.109 / §11.4.177 / §11.4.6 / §11.4.58 / §11.4.103 / §11.4.119 / §11.4.116 / §11.4.147. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-182-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.182`) + recommended gate `CM-TRACK-BRANCH-LABEL` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.182. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--skip-track-label`, `--unlabeled-agent-OK`, `--bare-work-stream-reference`, `--no-track-branch-prefix`, `--label-from-memory` flag.

**§11.4.166 — REPEALED (operator decision, 2026-06-22).** The Universal Semgrep static-analysis mandate is REPEALED — Semgrep is NO LONGER a mandatory requirement for projects governed by this Constitution. Static analysis / security scanning remains *encouraged* and may be re-adopted per project, but is NOT mandated, NOT a release blocker, NOT cascaded. Removed with the repeal: `scripts/semgrep/`, `scripts/hooks/semgrep_precommit.sh`, the `submodules/semgrep` submodule, the MCP/pre-commit/PATH wiring, the `.docs_chain/contexts/semgrep_status.yaml` context, and the `CM-COVENANT-114-166-PROPAGATION` / `CM-SEMGREP-WIRED` gates. Anchor number `11.4.166` is RETIRED (not reused); repealed before full fleet cascade — consuming projects never received it as a binding mandate. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.166.

**§11.4.167 — Big-work-item feature work-stream lifecycle (own CoW project copy + own branch/tags + per-feature builds, no-merge-until-approved, trunk-merged-into-every-stream) (User mandate, 2026-06-23).** Every BIG work item (new feature OR drastic/large fix) MUST be developed as its own isolated feature work-stream (ALL hold): (A) one big item = one feature work-stream in a sibling project copy (`<project>_<slug>`, slug lowercase §11.4.29; small changes stay on the trunk); (B) disk-feasible duplication MANDATORY (reflink/CoW clone on btrfs/XFS/ZFS/APFS, or `git worktree` + externalized build output) — a naive full deep copy / `git clone` per stream that would exhaust free space is FORBIDDEN, ~0-disk cost verified as captured evidence (§11.4.69/§11.4.6); per-stream `out/`, one shared compiler cache; (C) own `feature/<slug>` branch + own feature tags (`<base>-feat-<slug>[-<iter>]`, greppable §11.4.151), NEVER merged to trunk until the operator MANUALLY approves after §11.4.40 GREEN + §11.4.41 merge-first + §11.4.113 ff-only; (D) trunk merged INTO every live stream frequently (≥ after every trunk tag / daily, `git merge` never rebase) or flagged stale; (E) feature branch+tag cascades to EVERY touched submodule at the same HEAD, ff-only-pushed, untouched submodules stay trunk-pinned; (F) single-builder FIFO build queue + finite-device exclusive test queue (§11.4.119 / §11.4.58 L1 / §12.7 / §12.8), GC idle streams' regenerable output (§11.4.77); (G) every change crosses the full review + impact-research + anti-bluff gauntlet (§11.4.142 / §11.4.125 / §11.4.134 / §11.4.145) — a stream is NOT a quality carve-out; (H) resumable, data-safe lifecycle via a stream registry (§11.4.116 / §11.4.147), atomic-on-success clone, §9.2 pre-op backup on retire (unmerged work blocks auto-deletion), §12 / §12.6 bounds. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): guarantees isolation / disk-feasibility / greppable identity / controlled trunk↔feature merge — NOT any stream's correctness (still §11.4.108 + §11.4.40). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-167-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.167`) + recommended gates `CM-FEATURE-WORKSTREAM-COW-CLONE` / `CM-FEATURE-WORKSTREAM-NO-MERGE-UNTIL-APPROVED` / `CM-FEATURE-WORKSTREAM-TRUNK-SYNC-CADENCE` / `CM-FEATURE-WORKSTREAM-SUBMODULE-CASCADE` + paired §1.1 mutations. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.167. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--full-clone-per-feature`, `--deep-copy-stream`, `--skip-cow-clone`, `--merge-feature-without-approval`, `--no-trunk-sync`, `--skip-submodule-cascade`, `--unbounded-parallel-builds`, `--shared-device-no-lock`, `--retire-unmerged-stream`, `--feature-stream-quality-carveout` flag.

**§11.4.168 — Exported-document independent content + textual + full-visual validation mandate (User mandate, 2026-06-23).** Forensic FACT (2026-06-23): a "green" Mermaid export shipped RAW gantt-diagram source (`gantt`/`title`/`dateFormat`/`section`/`:done,`) as plain body text into user-facing PDFs; validation grepped the HTML for `class="mermaid"` but NEVER opened the exported PDF — the §11.4.108 SOURCE→ARTIFACT gap at the doc-export layer. Every generated/exported document (HTML/PDF/DOCX, §11.4.65 scope + §11.4.153 four-format set) MUST pass INDEPENDENT validation by a reviewer structurally separate from the generator (§11.4.70 / §11.4.20 / §11.4.142; NEVER generator self-check, §11.4.92 precedes never satisfies), run on BOTH source Markdown AND every exported artifact, across THREE layers ALL of which MUST hold: (1) CONTENT — nothing dropped/truncated/reordered/garbled, every section/table/list/figure/link present + complete (the §11.4.5/§11.4.69 quality bar, not presence-only); (2) TEXTUAL — NO raw markup / diagram source (`mermaid`/`gantt`/`graph`/`flowchart`/`sequenceDiagram`/… /`:done,` task lines) / unrendered code-fence body leaking as readable text, detected by reading the exported artifact as text (`pdftotext` / rendered-DOM / DOCX-text); (3) FULL VISUAL — diagrams render as IMAGES not source, layout intact (no overlap/clip/cut-off/collapsed/blank), verified by RENDERING (`pdftotext` + `pdfimages` image-enumeration + `pdftoppm`→OCR §11.4.117 / §11.4.107(12) confidence + ROI). (4) Anti-bluff — validator self-validated golden-good/golden-bad (§11.4.107(10): a golden-bad seeded with raw gantt body text + a truncated table MUST FAIL), iterates to a clean GO per §11.4.134. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): confirms the exported artifact a reader opens is faithful + readable + visually-rendered — NOT that source content is itself correct, and does NOT replace the §11.4.65 mtime-parity freshness gate (§11.4.168 is the READABILITY/FIDELITY layer the mtime gate cannot see). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-168-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.168`) + recommended gate `CM-EXPORTED-DOC-VISUALLY-VALIDATED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.168. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--skip-visual-validation`, `--raw-source-in-pdf-ok`, `--textual-check-suffices`, `--self-validate-export`, `--diagram-source-as-text-ok` flag.

**§11.4.169 — Mandatory comprehensive test-type coverage with anti-bluff captured evidence (User mandate, 2026-06-25).** Verbatim (2026-06-25): "MANDATORY test types EACH project MUST have with coverage aiming to 100%... unit, integration, e2e, full automation, challenges, helix qa, ddos, security, stress and chaos, concurrency (atomicy), race conditions or deadlocks, memory, bechmarking." Every project MUST be covered by this CLOSED ENUMERATED test-type set, each driven to as-close-to-100% as the domain permits, every PASS backed by rock-solid captured PHYSICAL evidence (§11.4.5 / §11.4.69 / §11.4.107), zero false results / zero bluff (§11.4 / §11.4.1 / §11.4.6) — the strict enumerated expansion of §11.4.27. The set (each REQUIRED where the domain warrants; only an honest §11.4.3 SKIP-with-reason for genuinely-absent topology/hardware/credential is permitted, NEVER a silent gap): (1) Unit (ONLY layer mocks/stubs/fakes permitted §11.4.27(A)); (2) Integration (real components, infra on-demand via the containers submodule §11.4.76 / §11.4.161 rootless); (3) e2e; (4) Full-automation (autonomous, re-runnable, no manual intervention §11.4.25 / §11.4.52 / §11.4.98, deterministic §11.4.50); (5) Challenges (`vasic-digital/challenges` anti-bluff banks); (6) HelixQA (`helix_qa` submodule test banks + fully-autonomous QA sessions); (7) DDoS / load-flood; (8) Security (authn/authz, injection/taint, secret-leak §11.4.10, crypto, CVEs, default-deny; security submodule); (9) Stress + Chaos (§11.4.85); (10) Concurrency / atomicity; (11) Race-condition / deadlock (race detector + lock-order); (12) Memory (leak census / soak, peak-RSS ceilings); (13) Benchmarking / performance (p50/p95/p99 vs baseline). Four-layer §11.4.4(b) enforcement of the suite + per-type paired §1.1 mutation; the coverage ledger (§11.4.25 / §11.4.52) classifies every feature × type × evidence-state — a missing required type or an `OPERATOR_ATTENDED_ONLY` row is a release blocker until promoted or honestly SKIP-justified. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-169-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.169`) + recommended gate `CM-MANDATORY-TEST-TYPES-COVERED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.169. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--skip-test-type`, `--partial-coverage-ok`, `--evidence-optional`, `--challenges-not-applicable`, `--skip-helixqa`, `--no-chaos`, `--no-ddos`, `--skip-memory-test`, `--skip-race-detector`, `--bench-optional` flag.

**§11.4.170 — Device-independent host-side rendered-UI visual-proof mandate (User mandate, 2026-06-25).** Every change to any user-facing UI surface (screen/component/view/widget/layout/theme on any platform — Android-Compose, iOS-SwiftUI/UIKit, web, desktop, TUI) MUST be proven by DEVICE-INDEPENDENT host-side RENDERED PIXELS before it may be claimed correct: the actual component rendered to a PNG ON THE HOST (NO device, NO emulator, NO running app; Compose→Roborazzi/Paparazzi, web→Playwright/Storybook, SwiftUI→snapshot-testing, equiv per stack) for EVERY `screen × state × {light,dark}` theme, dual-validated by (i) golden image-diff AND (ii) an OCR/vision oracle reading rendered text + labels + control bounds (NO overlap / label-over-label / clipping / off-screen / collapsed-or-giant-unbounded widget — the §11.4.162 layout invariants PROVEN on real pixels). Forbidden bluff (forensic FACT 2026-06-25): UI "validated" by VALUE/token/property-equality unit tests (a hex colour string, an sp/dp integer, a design-token field == a constant) that NEVER RENDERED A PIXEL stayed GREEN while the operator opened a broken giant-button screen — value/token/property-equality UI tests are FORBIDDEN as the PROOF a UI is correct (may SUPPLEMENT, NEVER SUBSTITUTE the rendered-pixel proof); a green UI suite with no rendered-pixel artefact for the changed surface is a §11.4 PASS-bluff. ALL hold: rendered-pixel proof per screen×state×theme, run on EVERY commit with zero hardware; dual oracle both required, each PASS citing the captured PNG + diff (§11.4.5/§11.4.69); a value-only UI claim is a §11.4.4 finding → render → fix → re-render GREEN; self-validated analyzer golden-good/golden-bad (§11.4.107(10)), thresholds on the project's OWN fixtures (§11.4.6); "device offline" is NEVER a valid skip (host-render IS the device-independent path); genuine no-host-render-harness ⇒ honest §11.4.3 SKIP + tracked migration item, never a value-only fallback. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): host-render proves the component renders correctly device-independently on every commit — it COMPLEMENTS not replaces §11.4.153/§11.4.158/§11.4.159/§11.4.160 live-device recording + §11.4.162 OpenDesign tokens + §11.4.168 exported-doc visual validation. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-170-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.170`) + recommended gate `CM-HOST-RENDERED-UI-VISUAL-PROOF` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.170. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--value-assertion-proves-ui`, `--skip-rendered-pixel-proof`, `--token-equality-suffices`, `--device-offline-skip-visual`, `--single-theme-only`, `--unvalidated-image-diff-OK`, `--no-ocr-layout-oracle` flag.

**§11.4.171 — Mandatory comprehensive human-readable workable-item descriptions (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** Every workable item (ATM-NNN ticket) in the project's workable-items database, Issues.md, Fixed.md, Issues_Summary.md, Fixed_Summary.md, and ALL derived documents MUST carry a comprehensive human-readable description in plain, non-technical language suitable for non-developers (project managers, stakeholders, team leads, business partners) — ≥ 5-7 sentences covering (a) WHAT it is (feature/fix/task in simple terms); (b) WHY it matters (user/business value); (c) HOW it works (mechanism, no code references); (d) WHO benefits; (e) the expected measurable outcome. Jargon, unexpanded acronyms, code references, and implementation details are FORBIDDEN as the primary explanation (technical detail may appear as supplementary context AFTER the plain-language explanation). An item without a human-readable description is a §11.4 documentation-layer violation. The `description` column in the SQLite DB (`docs/workable_items.db`) is the SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH; all derived documents carry the SAME description text. Gate `CM-HUMAN-READABLE-DESCRIPTION` (when implemented) asserts every item's `description` exists, non-empty, ≥ 50 characters; paired §1.1 mutation strips a description → gate FAILs. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.15 / §11.4.16 / §11.4.19 / §11.4.91 / §11.4.93 / §11.4.148 / §11.4.65. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-171-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.171`) + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.171. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.172 — Mandatory production-readiness planning with realistic timeline projection (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** Every project under this Constitution MUST maintain a living production-readiness planning document that: (a) provides REALISTIC timeline projections for all milestones (MVP, beta, production-ready) based on actual development velocity data (items completed per week, reopening rate, blocking dependencies); (b) identifies ALL danger zones, weaknesses, and risk areas with mitigation strategies; (c) accounts for HW-delivery timelines, licensing delays, and external-dependency risks; (d) defines the critical path and which items can slip without affecting MVP; (e) includes workstation/build-capacity analysis + optimization recommendations; (f) is updated at least monthly or whenever the item count changes by ≥ 10%; (g) is cross-referenced against the workable-items database for accuracy. The document lives at `docs/research/production_planning_<YYYYMMDD>/ANALYSIS.md` with HTML+PDF exports per §11.4.65. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): projections are velocity-based estimates — they guarantee sound methodology, NOT that specific dates will be met. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.6 / §11.4.40 / §11.4.42 / §11.4.93 / §11.4.108. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-172-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.172`) + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.172. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.173 — Containerized + distributed build mandate (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** EVERY build of EVERY component (source compile, artifact/package/installer/container-image production, codegen, asset render — for ANY language/platform: Go, Android/Gradle, desktop, web, native, firmware) MUST run INSIDE a specialized build container provisioned via the `digital.vasic.containers` submodule (§11.4.76) — NEVER on the bare host. The build containers MUST be DISTRIBUTED to the designated remote build host(s) via the SAME containers-submodule distribution mechanism (remote compose over SSH §11.4.76, rootless §11.4.161) so the build EXECUTES on the remote host (offloading the developer/main host); once complete the produced artifacts MUST be brought BACK to the originating host (scp/rsync/volume copy) for use/flashing/distribution. Building outside a container, or on the bare host, is FORBIDDEN — a release blocker (the "works on my machine" / unreproducible-build class). Build-host target + build-container definitions are config-injected (§11.4.28, never hardcoded in the submodule); a missing build-container capability is added by EXTENDING the containers submodule upstream (§11.4.74), never an ad-hoc host build. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): the containerized + distributed build guarantees reproducibility + host-isolation + capacity offload — it does NOT replace the §11.4.40 full-suite retest, §11.4.108 artifact→runtime verification, or §11.4.38 installable-asset evidence on the brought-back artifact. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.76 / §11.4.161 / §11.4.74 / §11.4.28 / §11.4.24 / §11.4.82 / §11.4.121 / §11.4.38 / §11.4.108 / §12.6. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-173-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.173`) + recommended gate `CM-CONTAINERIZED-DISTRIBUTED-BUILD` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.173. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--build-on-host`, `--skip-container-build`, `--local-build-ok`, `--no-distributed-build`, `--bare-host-build` flag.

**§11.4.174 — Shared-host process-ownership verification mandate (User mandate, 2026-06-29).** Verbatim operator mandate: "Make sure that processes we are checking are always OURS! ... on every host there may be other work being done!" On ANY host where concurrent work from other projects / users / agents may run (the normal case — a shared developer workstation), EVERY inspection of, conclusion about, or action on a process, build, daemon, port, lock-file, or system-state signal MUST FIRST positively VERIFY the target is OURS before drawing a diagnosis or acting. A diagnosis based on another project's process is a §11.4.6 guessing error; KILLING / signalling / restarting / altering a process that is NOT positively ours is a §12 + §11.4.133 safety violation (operator-workload destruction) — forbidden. Forensic FACT (2026-06-29): a 200%-CPU `java` + `gradlew` on the shared host was nearly mis-attributed to our build but was a separate `catalogizer` project's gradle test (`cwd=Projects/catalogizer`); a naive `pgrep java`/`gradle` would have matched it as "ours." ALL hold: (a) positive-ownership discriminator REQUIRED — attribute to us ONLY via a strong signal: `cwd` resolving inside THIS project's tree, `argv` naming our scripts/artifacts/repo path, a PID we launched + recorded (§11.4.147 registry), or a lock/port/socket path under our tree; a loose name match (`pgrep java`/`gradle`/`node`/`python`/`podman`/`zig`) is NEVER sufficient; (b) NEVER kill/signal/restart a process not positively ours — other projects' daemons/pods are off-limits; the §12.8 `pkill -f GradleDaemon` remediation MUST be scoped to OUR daemons (cwd/argv under our tree), never host-wide; (c) contention → surface, don't break (§11.4.66 / §11.4.101), keep progressing non-blocked work; (d) every `pgrep`/`ps` filter MUST exclude the checking command's OWN argv AND other-project matches, preferring our absolute repo path; (e) applies to ALL state (ports, lock files, caches, pods, tmux sessions, temp files), not just processes. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): ownership-verified inspection prevents mis-attribution + cross-project damage — it does not itself prove our process is healthy. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.6 / §11.4.101 / §11.4.66 / §11.4.147 / §12 / §12.8 / §11.4.133. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-174-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.174`) + recommended gate `CM-PROCESS-OWNERSHIP-VERIFIED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.174. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--assume-process-ours`, `--loose-pgrep-ok`, `--kill-any-matching-process`, `--skip-ownership-check` flag.

**§11.4.176 — Conflict-free multi-track work-division + exactly-once claim registry + capability-aware deadlock-proof device-lock (User mandate, 2026-07-02).** When a project runs multiple concurrent work-STREAM tracks (§11.4.167 / §11.4.58 / §11.4.103) sharing (a) a common pool of workable items and (b) a scarce pool of exclusive hardware/resources, TWO cooperating arbitration layers are MANDATORY, both conflict-free BY CONSTRUCTION: **(A) work-item layer — exactly-once claim registry** — every workable item OR logical GROUP of items sharing files/subsystem/feature/schema is assigned to AT MOST ONE track at a time via a lock-arbitrated append-only claim registry (extends §11.4.147 + §11.4.116); claim-before-touch, a second claim on an already-claimed item is DENIED; logical groups are claimed WHOLE (disjoint file-scope §11.4.58 L3 + per-track worktree/CoW §11.4.167 = tracks physically cannot touch the same bytes); no codebase loss (§9.2 backups / §11.4.113 ff-only-merge-onto-latest-main NEVER force-push / §11.4.84 quiescence / §11.4.41 merge-first); results ALWAYS produced (abandoned claim TTL-expires back to the pool). **(B) hardware layer — capability-aware deadlock-proof device-lock** — when N tracks outnumber M exclusive devices, exactly ONE track owns each device (§11.4.119); a track leases ONE OR MORE devices selected by required CAPABILITY (not merely identity); the arbiter is DEADLOCK-FREE by breaking all four Coffman conditions (hold-and-wait eliminated — multi-device acquire is ALL-OR-NOTHING in one critical section; circular-wait eliminated — acquire is NON-BLOCKING, wins the whole set or returns EBUSY; no-preemption relaxed — lease TTL + heartbeat + reap so a crashed holder's lease auto-expires §11.4.147; the only lock held is a short bounded flock over the atomic check-and-claim); registry = append-only JSONL + atomically-rewritten snapshot (§11.4.116). **(C) universal decoupling + evidence-based resource-tuning** — both layers universal/decoupled/project-not-aware (§11.4.17/§11.4.28/§11.4.35); resource-tuning decisions (stream count, per-stream memory §12.6, lease breadth, queue depth §11.4.167) MUST be EVIDENCE-BASED (§11.4.24 / §11.4.5), never guessed (§11.4.6). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.6/§11.4.17/§11.4.24/§11.4.28/§11.4.35/§11.4.41/§11.4.58/§11.4.84/§11.4.85/§11.4.103/§11.4.113/§11.4.116/§11.4.119/§11.4.147/§11.4.167/§12.6/§9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-176-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.176`) + recommended gates `CM-WORK-DIVISION-EXCLUSIVE-CLAIM` / `CM-NO-CROSS-TRACK-SCOPE-OVERLAP` / `CM-LOGICAL-GROUP-COHESION` / `CM-DEVICE-LOCK-DEADLOCK-FREE` + paired §1.1 mutations. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.176. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--allow-cross-track-overlap`, `--skip-claim-registry`, `--split-logical-group`, `--blocking-device-acquire`, `--allow-partial-device-hold`, `--tune-resources-by-guess` flag.

**§11.4.177 — Developer-tooling project-decoupling + invocation-directory operation (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** No project-specific script / hook / alias / binary may be wired — copied, symlinked, PATH-exported, or aliased — into a global or shared developer-tooling PATH; shared tooling MUST be project-agnostic and operate on the INVOCATION directory (cwd, or an explicit path/config argument), NEVER a hardcoded project path. A project-specific helper lives in + runs from its own repo; a genuinely-reusable helper is promoted to the shared toolkit ONLY after being stripped of every project-specific assumption (paths, device serials, package names, region endpoints) and taking its target from the invocation context. A project script reachable on the global/shared PATH is a decoupling violation of equal severity to importing project-specific code into a shared submodule (§11.4.28). Forensic FACT (2026-07-04): a project cwd-hook symlinked into the global Claude-Toolkit PATH re-coupled every alias to one hardcoded checkout. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): decoupling guarantees the tool is project-agnostic — NOT that it is correct (that still needs the tool's own tests). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.28 / §11.4.29 / §11.4.35 / §11.4.11 / §11.4.6. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-177-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.177`) + recommended gate `CM-TOOLING-PROJECT-DECOUPLED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.177. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--global-symlink-ok`, `--hardcode-project-path`, `--wire-into-shared-path` flag.

**§11.4.178 — Track-qualified identity for parallel work streams (session-name collision ban) (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** Parallel work streams that share hardware, a git backing store, a tmux/session namespace, a lock namespace, or any single-owner resource MUST be addressed by a TRACK-QUALIFIED identity (`<project>__<track>__<role>`), NEVER a bare directory basename. Multiple checkouts/clones/worktrees sharing basename `atmosphere` collapse into one session/lock/log key and cross-wire tmux targets, lock files, device claims, and log directories (the observed collision, 2026-07-04). Every registry row, session name, lock path, log directory, and device claim MUST carry the track-qualified key; a bare-basename identity for a resource with ≥ 2 concurrent claimants is a violation. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): a unique identity prevents cross-wiring — it does not itself arbitrate ownership (that is §11.4.119 + §11.4.176, the multi-track work-division + exactly-once-claim + device-lock arbitration anchor). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.111 / §11.4.119 / §11.4.176 / §11.4.29 / §11.4.58. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-178-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.178`) + recommended gate `CM-TRACK-QUALIFIED-IDENTITY` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.178. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--bare-basename-ok`, `--skip-track-qualifier`, `--shared-session-name` flag.

**§11.4.179 — Corruption-isolated parallel git streams (own-.git independent clones, not shared-common-dir worktrees) (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** When corruption-isolation is a requirement, parallel git work streams MUST each be an isolated repository with its OWN `.git` (own object store, own index, own lock namespace), NOT `git worktree` checkouts sharing one common `.git`. A shared common-dir is a single point of failure: one stale `index.lock` / `.commit_all.lock` / `.push_all.lock` freezes EVERY stream at once (the observed 9-h all-track freeze, 2026-07-04), and one corrupted object store loses every stream. Each stream's `git rev-parse --git-common-dir` MUST resolve INSIDE the stream's own tree; a common-dir resolving to a shared parent is a violation. Where CoW/reflink disk-feasibility is the constraint, use the §11.4.167 reflink-clone-with-own-`.git` path (a btrfs/XFS/ZFS/APFS reflink shares extents on disk while keeping a per-stream `.git`, so isolation and disk-feasibility both hold). Honest boundary (§11.4.6): own-`.git` isolation contains lock/corruption blast radius — it does NOT remove per-repo stale-lock reaping (§11.4.180) nor ff-only no-force integration (§11.4.113). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.167 / §11.4.119 / §11.4.176 / §11.4.58 / §9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-179-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.179`) + recommended gate `CM-GIT-STREAMS-OWN-COMMON-DIR` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.179. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--shared-common-git`, `--worktree-when-isolation-required`, `--skip-git-isolation` flag.

**§11.4.180 — Commit/push (single-writer) wrappers MUST auto-reap provably-stale locks before acquiring (User mandate, 2026-07-04).** Every commit / push / single-writer wrapper MUST, before acquiring its own lock, auto-reap any PROVABLY-stale git lock — one whose recorded holder PID is DEAD (`kill -0` fails), OR (no PID recorded) older than a defined threshold AND with no live wrapper/git process holding that repo. The reap covers the wrapper's own lock plus the git-internal existence-based locks (`index.lock`, `HEAD.lock`, `refs/**/*.lock`) that git does NOT auto-release on holder death. It MUST NEVER remove a lock whose holder is ALIVE (removing a live-held lock corrupts a concurrent writer — §9.2). Each reap decision (REAPED / KEPT + reason) is logged as captured evidence (§11.4.6 — liveness PROVEN via `kill -0`, never assumed). A wrapper that blocks indefinitely on a dead-holder lock (the observed 9-h freeze, 2026-07-04) is a violation. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): reaping clears dead-holder deadlock — it does NOT substitute for the own-`.git` isolation of §11.4.179 (which shrinks the blast radius from all-streams to one). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.84 / §11.4.88 / §11.4.6 / §9.2 / §11.4.116 / §11.4.179. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-180-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.180`) + recommended gate `CM-WRAPPER-STALE-LOCK-AUTO-REAP` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.180. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--skip-stale-lock-reap`, `--force-remove-live-lock`, `--block-on-dead-holder` flag.

**§11.4.181 — Consistent controlled feature-branch naming: one feature/logic-group ⇒ exactly ONE canonical branch name across the main repo + all owned submodules (User mandate, 2026-07-05).** Verbatim (2026-07-05): "System MUST pay attention not to create multiple feat. branches with different names for one same feature or group of workable items / features! Naming MUST BE consistent and carefully controlled!" One feature / logical group of workable items MUST map to EXACTLY ONE canonical branch name, used IDENTICALLY on the main repo AND every touched owned submodule — NEVER two differently-named branches for one feature/group, NEVER per-repo naming drift. ALL hold: (1) **single canonical name per group** minted ONCE per the §11.4.167 D scheme (`feature/<slug>` branch + `<prefix>-<base>-feat-<slug>` tag, `<slug>` lowercase snake/kebab §11.4.29), used identically across the main repo + every branched submodule (an untouched submodule stays on its base branch, NOT force-branched); (2) **single source of truth** — the canonical name is recorded ONCE in the §11.4.176 exactly-once claim registry / the §11.4.93 workable-items `logic_group → branch` mapping and LOOKED UP, never re-invented (creating a branch whose name ≠ the group's registered canonical name, OR minting a 2nd name for a group that already has one, is a §11.4.6 no-guessing violation); (3) **mechanical enforcement** (§11.4.75) — gate `CM-BRANCH-NAME-CONSISTENCY` FAILs on an unregistered feature-branch name / two divergent names for one group / a submodule branch diverging from the group's main-repo canonical name, paired §1.1 mutation (register one group under two divergent names → gate FAILs); (4) **risk-free reconciliation** (§9.2 / §11.4.113 / §11.4.84) — a mis-named/duplicate branch is reconciled by MERGING its commits onto the canonical branch (union, no `-s ours`/rebase/reset that drops commits, `git log <canonical>..<misnamed>` empty after merge, no conflict markers), ff-only push to all upstreams (NEVER force-push), retiring the mis-named branch only after the merge is confirmed on all mirrors (delete-before-merge forbidden). Honest boundary (§11.4.6): "probably the same feature" is NOT a determination — bind the branch to a group via the registry, never guess. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.167 / §11.4.176 / §11.4.178 / §11.4.179 / §11.4.28 / §11.4.29 / §11.4.93 / §11.4.113 / §11.4.84 / §11.4.6 / §11.4.75 / §9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-181-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.181`) + recommended gate `CM-BRANCH-NAME-CONSISTENCY` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.181. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--allow-divergent-branch-names`, `--skip-branch-registry`, `--rename-branch-freely`, `--per-repo-branch-name-OK`, `--two-names-one-feature-OK` flag.

**§11.4.182 — Track+branch work-stream identity label `(T<N>/<branch> - <alias>)` on every agent/subagent label + every operator-facing work-stream reference (User mandate, 2026-07-05).** Operator mandate (2026-07-05): "EVERY agent/subagent/work-stream label AND every operator-facing report reference to a work stream MUST carry a `(T<N>/<branch> - <alias>)` prefix identifying the track + git branch + the claude-toolkit alias in use — e.g. `(T1/main - claude1) ATM-312 MPV drm_prime investigation`, `(T2/feat/mistiq-vader - deepseek) SPK-XXX ...`." In a multi-track layout (parallel checkouts each on a distinct branch and potentially driven by a distinct claude-toolkit alias — e.g. `/mnt/track1..4`) a bare work-stream label does not say WHICH track/branch/alias produced it, so cross-track dispatches, status reports, and progress lines collide and mislead. ALL hold: (1) **universal label form** — every agent / subagent / work-stream label AND every operator-facing reference (agent-dispatch descriptions, status reports, resume/handoff docs, progress lines) MUST START with a `(T<N>/<branch> - <alias>)` prefix; (2) **deterministic derivation, never guessed** (§11.4.6) — `<N>` from the checkout path (`/mnt/track<N>/…`; honest `?` when not under a numbered track, never a guessed number), `<branch>` from `git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD`, `<alias>` from the `CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR` basename `.claude-<alias>` → `<alias>` (honest `?` when unset/non-matching, never a guessed name) (reference labeler `scripts/multitrack/track_branch_label.sh`); (3) **mechanical enforcement** (§11.4.75 / §11.4.109-class) — a PreToolUse guard hook (`constitution/scripts/hooks/guard-track-branch-label.sh`, inherited BY REFERENCE per §11.4.177, never copied) BLOCKS any Agent/Task/TaskCreate dispatch whose `description` (or `subagent` label) does not START with `^\(T[0-9]+/[^ )]+ - [^ )]+\) ` (branch AND alias both required, both non-empty), non-agent tools untouched; pre-build gate `CM-TRACK-BRANCH-LABEL` asserts labeler + hook exist/executable/parseable, hook wired in runtime settings, convention doc exists; (4) **honest boundary** (§11.4.6) — a `?` in the track field OR the alias field is a valid honest label (unknown track / no git repo / no matching `CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR`), never a bluff; the enforced format surfaces (blocks) an off-track dispatch or a dispatch missing its alias segment rather than silently mislabeling it. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.178 (the label-prefix instantiation applied to EVERY agent/subagent label + operator-facing reference) / §11.4.29 / §11.4.75 / §11.4.109 / §11.4.177 / §11.4.6 / §11.4.58 / §11.4.103 / §11.4.119 / §11.4.116 / §11.4.147. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-182-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.182`) + recommended gate `CM-TRACK-BRANCH-LABEL` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.182. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--skip-track-label`, `--unlabeled-agent-OK`, `--bare-work-stream-reference`, `--no-track-branch-prefix`, `--label-from-memory` flag.

**§11.4.183 — Maximal multi-agent utilization per work-stream + full-constitution-application + zero-bluff mandate (User mandate, 2026-07-07).** Compact summary: every track / work-stream MUST maximize multi-agent working approaches — subagent-driven development (§11.4.20/§11.4.70), independent review agents (§11.4.125/§11.4.142/§11.4.165/§11.4.134), parallel background streams with auto-backfill (§11.4.58/§11.4.103), and every other applicable agent form — so every track produces the MOST completed work at the HIGHEST quality in the LEAST time; every track MUST apply the ENTIRE constitution (every rule, mandatory constraint, guide, and derived technology — NOTHING ignored, skipped, avoided, or deemed less-relevant); there MUST NEVER be false / faulty / untested / unverified results or bluff of any kind anywhere (§11.4 anti-bluff covenant, captured evidence §11.4.5/§11.4.69/§11.4.107); honest boundary §11.4.6 — "maximize agents" is bounded by §12.6 60% memory + §11.4.58 parallel-agent cap + genuine parallelizability + §11.4.119 single-resource-owner, spawning contending/redundant agents is NOT maximization, the bar is maximum USEFUL parallel throughput not agent count. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.20/.58/.70/.92/.94/.97/.103/.119/.125/.126/.134/.142/.165/§12.6. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-183-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.183`) + recommended gate `CM-MAX-AGENTS-PER-TRACK` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.183. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--single-agent-OK`, `--skip-review-agents`, `--partial-constitution-application`, `--serialise-parallelisable-work` flag.
**§11.4.184 — Mandatory SonarQube static-analysis CLI + local tooling installed and PATH-discoverable (User mandate, 2026-07-06).** Compact summary: every project/host that runs static analysis MUST have the SonarQube scanner CLI (`sonar-scanner`) installed AND durably PATH-discoverable via `.bashrc`/`.zshrc` (exactly like the Firebase/GitHub/GitLab CLIs), PLUS the shared `constitution/scripts/sonarqube/` tooling (`sonarqube_install_check.sh`/`sonarqube_lib.sh`/`sonarqube_run_scan.sh`/`sonarqube_container.sh`+`compose/`) consumed BY REFERENCE (§11.4.28/§11.4.177/§11.4.80-style, NEVER copied); proven GREEN by `sonarqube_install_check.sh` exit 0 + `command -v sonar-scanner` resolving (anti-bluff §11.4.6, never assumed); the local SonarQube server runs via rootless podman (§11.4.161), never rootful docker/sudo; DISTINCT from the repealed §11.4.166 Semgrep mandate — mandates TOOLING availability, not a scan on every build. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4.28/.36/.74/.75/.109/.161/.166/.177/.6. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-184-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.184`) + recommended gate `CM-SONARQUBE-CLI-INSTALLED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.184. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--skip-sonarqube-install`, `--sonar-cli-optional`, `--ad-hoc-sonar-path`, `--rootful-sonar-OK` flag.
**§11.4.185 — Manual QA-team testing as the mandatory FINAL confirmation of done (User mandate, 2026-07-07).** Compact summary: no set of features / scope of work / release may be considered fully completed until it has received MANUAL TESTING confirmation by the project's QA team as the FINAL confirmation step — EVERYWHERE and ALWAYS, never forgotten. Every automated gate (§11.4 anti-bluff, §11.4.5/§11.4.69 captured evidence, §11.4.52 autonomous validation, §11.4.40 full-suite retest, §11.4.108 four-layer verification, §11.4.132 risk-ordered validation) is NECESSARY but NOT SUFFICIENT — manual QA is the FINAL human sufficiency gate. Composition with §11.4.52 ADDS, never weakens: a feature MUST have BOTH the autonomous path (primary, always-on) AND the manual-QA final confirmation — automation-only with no QA sign-off is a §11.4.185 violation; manual-QA-only with no autonomous path is still a §11.4.52 violation. Workflow: autonomous-validation-GREEN → build → flash/deploy → autonomous on-device validation → HAND OFF to the QA team → ONLY after QA-team manual confirmation is the scope "fully completed"; the §11.4.126 autonomous-loop release-tag terminal condition now REQUIRES this confirmation before the tag is cut. Honest boundary (§11.4.6): the agent MUST hand off + WAIT for QA-team confirmation, never self-certify/simulate/infer it; while waiting the agent keeps progressing every OTHER non-blocked item in parallel (§11.4.87/.94/.97/.101) — the wait parks that one scope, not the loop. Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §11.4/.5/.6/.40/.52/.69/.108/.126/.129/.130/.132. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-185-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.185`) + recommended gate `CM-MANUAL-QA-FINAL-CONFIRMATION` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.185. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--automation-only-is-done`, `--skip-manual-qa`, `--self-certify-qa-confirmation`, `--infer-qa-from-automation` flag.
**§12.12 — Process/thread-limit (RLIMIT_NPROC) awareness for parallel subagent/multi-process work (User mandate, 2026-07-07).** Compact summary: heavy parallel subagent/multi-process work is bounded by the OS per-user process/thread limit `ulimit -u` (`RLIMIT_NPROC`), which on Linux counts ALL threads AND processes owned by the real UID, not per-process; ambient tooling (MCP servers, language runtimes) can consume most of the budget before project work starts (forensic FACT: a `ulimit -u 4096` host sat at ~3900-4005 threads from the ambient MCP fleet alone, leaving under 150 threads of headroom; a 4th Go-heavy subagent hit `EAGAIN`/`failed to create new OS thread`). Thread-limit exhaustion is a §12 host-safety event that YIELDS UNCONDITIONALLY, same standing as §12.6 (memory) and §12.7 (AOSP `-j` cap) — an ORTHOGONAL exhaustion axis, both MUST be checked independently before scaling parallelism. Mandatory pre-scale diagnosis: `ulimit -u`/`ulimit -Hu` (soft/hard) + live `ps -L --no-headers -u "$USER" | wc -l` thread count; headroom = soft minus live; signals (`EAGAIN`, `fork: retry`, `failed to create new OS thread`) never guessed, always captured (§11.4.6); low headroom → SERIALIZE, avoid `GOMAXPROCS=nproc`-class spikes. Raising the limit — three cited techniques: (a) `prlimit --pid <PID> --nproc=<soft>:<hard>` (root, no-restart); (b) `/etc/security/limits.conf`/systemd `LimitNPROC` (persistent, next-session); (c) self `ulimit -u <N>` up to the existing hard ceiling (current session) — `su -c` scope is transient only. Freeing threads by stopping non-essential tooling REQUIRES explicit operator authorization (§11.4.122, no-silent-removal); cmdline-pattern kill helpers MUST exclude the caller's own `$$`/`$PPID` (self-kill hazard). Classification: universal (§11.4.17). Composes §12/.6/.7/§11.4.58/.101/.103/.122/§9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-12-12-PROPAGATION` (literal `12.12`) + recommended gate `CM-NPROC-HEADROOM-CHECK` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §12.12. Non-compliance is a release blocker. No escape hatch — no `--ignore-thread-limit`, `--dispatch-blind`, `--skip-headroom-check`, `--autonomous-tooling-kill`, `--assume-ulimit-scope` flag.

**§11.4.186 — Anti-divergence enforcement: cross-document consistency is a mandatory-before-export/commit gate, never an after-the-fact audit (research-derived, 2026-07-08).** Concise summary: any project maintaining more than one representation of the same tracked data (plan + brief + workable-items DB + summaries + `.md`/`.html`/`.pdf`/`.docx` exports) MUST enforce cross-document consistency as a deterministic PASS/FAIL/SKIP gate that runs BEFORE any export render, any doc/DB sync `verify`, and any doc-set commit — never as an after-the-fact human audit. Five decidable check families (DEDUP/TIMELINE/CROSS-DOC/INTEGRITY/STRUCTURAL); §11.4.86 fingerprint re-arms on any input change; self-validated analyzer (golden-good/golden-bad/negative-control) per §11.4.107(10). Honest boundary: proves internal consistency, not plan correctness. Composes §11.4.6/.12/.33/.44/.50/.53/.54/.60/.65/.73/.75/.85/.86/.91/.93/.95/.106/.107/.108/.110/.148/.176. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-186-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.186`) + recommended gate `CM-DOC-INTEGRITY-VALIDATION` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.186. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.187 — Automatic multi-track ruler orchestration (User mandate, 2026-07-04; landed 2026-07-09).** Concise summary: multi-track parallel-development orchestration MUST ship as a universal, automatic, out-of-the-box, inherited engine (never a per-project reimplementation) at `constitution/scripts/multitrack/` — a single conductor session that spawns/resumes/monitors/controls per-track headless workers (native headless `claude -p --output-format stream-json`, session_id from the `init` event, success read from `result.is_error` never exit code), per-subscription auth + rate-limit fallback (unset ambient `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, rebind on 429), crash-resilient self-supervisor (durable state, write-temp-then-rename), idempotent bootstrap auto-invoked on every constitution pull. Project-agnostic engine; consumer supplies only per-host `config/multitrack/<hostname>.yaml` as data. Composes §11.4.20/.28/.58/.70/.101/.103/.111/.116/.119/.126/.128/.131/.147/.164/.167/.176/§12.6/§12.8. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-187-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.187`) + recommended gates `CM-MULTITRACK-ENGINE-IN-CONSTITUTION` / `CM-MULTITRACK-AUTOINSTALL-WIRED` / `CM-MULTITRACK-BOOTSTRAP-IDEMPOTENT` / `CM-MULTITRACK-BIND-ON-START` / `CM-MULTITRACK-FALLBACK-MONITOR` / `CM-MULTITRACK-HEADLESS-SPAWN` / `CM-MULTITRACK-RULER-SUPERVISOR` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.187. **§11.4.188 — Regular main→feature merge cadence: every track/feature-branch MUST FREQUENTLY merge canonical `main` into itself DURING the work, never only at the end (User mandate, 2026-07-09).** Concise summary: every long-lived feature branch AND every parallel-development track MUST regularly `git merge` (NEVER rebase) canonical `main`/`master` INTO itself THROUGHOUT the work — after every trunk tag, at minimum daily while live, and before starting significant new work — so the branch never drifts far and the eventual back-merge stays small and low-conflict. Fetch-first, §9.2 pre-op backup before large merges, resolve conflicts carefully (zero markers, zero dropped files), integrate only when quiescent (§11.4.84), never force-push after merge. Post-merge proof required: smoke gate GREEN + zero conflict-marker grep + no-lost-commit check. Generalises §11.4.167(D) from big feature-streams to every branch. Composes §9/.9.2/.37/.41/.42/.71/.84/.88/.89/.103/.113/.167/.176/.178/.179/.181. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-188-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.188`) + recommended gate `CM-REGULAR-MAIN-MERGE-INTO-FEATURE` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.188. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.189 — Most-reopened cases get extra-depth live-testing scrutiny FIRST (User mandate, 2026-07-10).** Concise summary: all live testing (on-device/on-target runtime validation) MUST give the cases with the HIGHEST §11.4.55 reopens-count extra-depth retest, re-investigation per §11.4.102/§11.4.146, and full rock-solid physical-evidence confirmation (§11.4.5/.69/.107/.123) — scrutinised FIRST, ahead of the rest of the live-test suite. Strengthens §11.4.132(d) (most-reopened as ranking factor) into its own extra-depth mandate at the live-test layer. Composes §11.4.5/.6/.55/.69/.102/.107/.108/.115/.123/.129/.130/.132/.135/.146. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.190 — Website engineering-quality mandate: every project website MUST be fully responsive + completely SEO-optimized + uniquely OpenDesign-authored + bleeding-edge enterprise-quality, each PROVEN with captured evidence (User mandate, 2026-07-10).** Concise summary: every website/web-UI surface a project ships — INCLUDING the project's own website — MUST satisfy AND PROVE with captured physical evidence (never a bare claim): (A) full responsiveness across all browser engines/OSes/device classes/screen sizes with no broken layout at any breakpoint; (B) complete SEO optimization (semantic HTML, meta/OG/Twitter cards, canonical URLs, structured data, sitemap/robots, WCAG AA, Core Web Vitals); (C) unique OpenDesign-token-authored templates (§11.4.162), never generic/off-the-shelf; (D) bleeding-edge enterprise visual quality in both light and dark themes. Proof required per facet: host-rendered cross-breakpoint screenshots + layout oracle, automated SEO audit meeting a score floor, OpenDesign-token provenance, §11.4.170 device-independent pixel proof. Strict web expansion of §11.4.162 + binds §11.4.170; sibling of §11.4.168. Composes §11.4.5/.6/.69/.107/.162/.168/.170. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.191 — Work-to-track/branch binding enforcement: a logic-group's work can NEVER be committed OR dispatched onto the wrong track/branch (research-derived, 2026-07-10).** Concise summary: every logical group of workable items binds to EXACTLY ONE canonical `(track, branch)` recorded ONCE in the single source of truth (the §11.4.93 workable-items DB `logic_groups.destination` + `canonical_track` + `group_paths` file-scope manifest); no change belonging to a group may LAND on or be DISPATCHED to a different track/branch. File-scope generalisation of §11.4.181/.182 branch-name consistency to work-PLACEMENT consistency. Preventive PreToolUse guard `guard-work-track-binding.sh` (inherited by reference, fail-closed) BLOCKS mis-placed commits/dispatches; detective gate `CM-WORK-TRACK-BINDING-ENFORCED` audits added commits on the current branch. Mis-placed changes reconciled by MERGE onto the canonical branch (never force-push, never commit-loss). Composes §11.4.6/.28/.29/.35/.58/.75/.84/.93/.95/.109/.110/.113/.119/.167/.176/.177/.178/.181/.182/§9.2. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-191-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.191`) + recommended gate `CM-WORK-TRACK-BINDING-ENFORCED` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.191. Non-compliance is a release blocker.

**§11.4.192 — Continuous multi-track auto-backfill: a FREE track MUST be IMMEDIATELY re-assigned its next-highest-priority domain work-set, never left idle while its domain has actionable items (User mandate, 2026-07-11).** Concise summary: the moment any track's worker COMPLETES its current work-set, that FREE track MUST be IMMEDIATELY assigned the NEXT-highest-priority actionable work-set from its own domain (§11.4.191 logic_group/canonical branch), claimed exactly-once (§11.4.176 registry), dispatched as a new §11.4.182-labelled stream — no waiting for a scheduled wake or operator prompt. When the next item's on-device validation is gated (pending build/device/manual-QA), the track still advances the item's SOURCE-SIDE work and honestly SKIPs only the device-gated validation portion. Promotes §11.4.103(B) auto-backfill from the STREAM layer to the TRACK layer. A track idles ONLY when its domain has genuinely zero remaining actionable items or every remaining item is externally blocked with no source-side advancement possible — "merges are done" is NEVER a valid idle reason. Composes §11.4.42/.58/.72/.94/.97/.101/.103/.167/.176/.178/.179/.182/.187. Propagation gate `CM-COVENANT-114-192-PROPAGATION` (literal `11.4.192`) + recommended gate `CM-CONTINUOUS-MULTITRACK-BACKFILL` + paired §1.1 mutation. **Canonical authority:** constitution submodule [`Constitution.md`](constitution/Constitution.md) §11.4.192. Non-compliance is a release blocker.
